11/04/25, 2:53â€¯pm - Vaibhav(Jaadu): # Frequency of each remainder
    remainder_count = [0] * k
    
    for num in s:
        remainder_count[num % k] += 1

    # Start with at most one element divisible by k
    count = min(remainder_count[0], 1)

    # Check from 1 to k//2 (excluding k/2 if k even)
    for i in range(1, (k // 2) + 1):
        if i != k - i:
            count += max(remainder_count[i], remainder_count[k - i])
        else:
            # For the special case when k is even and i == k-i
            count += 1

    return count

02/05/25, 3:04â€¯pm - Vaibhav(Jaadu): def getMinimumCost(k, c):
    c.sort(reverse=True)  # Step 1: Sort prices descending
    total_cost = 0

    for i in range(len(c)):
        # The multiplier is how many flowers this customer has bought already
        multiplier = i // k + 1
        total_cost += multiplier * c[i]

    return total_cost
02/05/25, 3:06â€¯pm - Vaibhav(Jaadu): def luckBalance(k, contests):
    important = []
    total_luck = 0

    for luck, importance in contests:
        if importance == 1:
            important.append(luck)
        else:
            total_luck += luck

    important.sort(reverse=True)

    total_luck += sum(important[:k])

    total_luck -= sum(important[k:])

    return total_luck
02/05/25, 3:08â€¯pm - Vaibhav(Jaadu): def stones(n, a, b):
    results = set()

    for i in range(n):
        value = a * (n - 1 - i) + b * i
        results.add(value)

    return sorted(results)

14/05/25, 12:05â€¯pm - Vaibhav Pandey: from abc import ABC, abstractmethod

class BankAccount(ABC):
    def init(self, initial_balance=0):
        self.__balance = initial_balance  # private variable

    @abstractmethod
    def deposit(self, amount):
        pass

    @abstractmethod
    def withdraw(self, amount):
        pass

    @abstractmethod
    def check_balance(self):
        pass

# Concrete class implementing the abstract methods
class MyBankAccount(BankAccount):
    def deposit(self, amount):
        if amount > 0:
            self.BankAccount_balance += amount
            print(f"Deposited: {amount}")
        else:
            print("Invalid deposit amount.")

    def withdraw(self, amount):
        if amount <= 0:
            print("Invalid withdrawal amount.")
        elif amount > self.BankAccount_balance:
            print("Insufficient funds.")
        else:
            self.BankAccount_balance -= amount
            print(f"Withdrawn: {amount}")

    def check_balance(self):
        return self.BankAccount_balance

    a=MyBankAccount(10000)

a.withdraw(4000)
a.deposit(2000)

12/06/25, 10:37â€¯am - Vaibhav(Jaadu): import java.util.*;

public class Utils2 {
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
		/*object o1=new ArrayList<String>();
		o1 can hold all types of objects
		List l1=new ArrayList<String>();// it can hold linked lists too
		base type of reference is good as if the object is killed then reference variable lasts till end.
		ArrayList<String> l2=new ArrayList<String>();// it cannot hold linedlist
		*/
        List l1=new ArrayList<String>();
        System.out.println("Initial size of l1 is : "+ l1.size());
        l1.add("A");
        l1.add("M");
        l1.add("B");
        System.out.println("New Size of l1 is : "+ l1.size());
        System.out.println("l1 contains : "+l1);
        l1.add(2,"k");
        System.out.println("Now l1 contains : "+l1);
        //l1.add(l1);
        //System.out.println("after adding l1, l1 contains : "+l1);
        // o/p : l1 contains : [A, M, k, B, (this Collection)]
        // we can't give object reference using this keyword
        //l1.addAll(l1);
        //System.out.println("Using addAll, Now l1 contains : "+l1);
        List l2=new ArrayList<String>();
        l2.add(l1);
        System.out.println("l2 contains : "+l2);
        // creates list inside list
        l2.addAll(l1);
        System.out.println("Now l2 contains : "+l2);

        

    }

}

21/07/25, 9:22â€¯pm - Mahi: @867051314767696 gussa ko control krne ke tips btao..
21/07/25, 9:22â€¯pm - Meta AI: Gussa ko control karne ke liye yeh tips apna sakte hain:

1. *Gahri saans lene ka abhyaas*: Jab aapko gussa aaye, toh gahri saans lein. Yeh aapke dimaag ko shant karne mein madad karta hai.

2. *Thoda break lein*: Agar aapko lagta hai ki aap gusse mein kuch galat kar sakte hain, toh thoda break lein. Kisi shant jagah par jaakar baith jayein aur apne vicharon ko samjhne ki koshish karein.

3. *Vyayam karein*: Niyamit vyayam aapke manasik sthiti ko behtar banata hai aur gusse ko kam karta hai.

4. *Sakaratmak soch*: Apne vicharon ko sakaratmak banane ki koshish karein. Gusse ke samay, apne aap ko yaad dilayein ki gussa karne se kuch nahi hoga.

5. *Samay par neend*: Paryapt neend lena bahut zaroori hai. Neend ki kami se aap chidchide ho sakte hain.

6. *Dhyan aur yoga*: Dhyan aur yoga aapke man ko shant karne mein madad karte hain aur aapko gusse ko control karne mein sahayak hote hain.

7. *Apne aap se baat karein*: Jab aapko gussa aaye, toh apne aap se baat karein aur apne aap ko shant karne ki salah dein.

8. *Kisi dost ya parivaar wale se baat karein*: Apne gusse ke baare mein kisi vishwasniya vyakti se baat karein. Kabhi-kabhi apne dil ki baat nikalne se aapko behatar feel hota hai.

In tips ko apnakar aap apne gusse ko control kar sakte hain aur apne jeevan ko behatar bana sakte hain. ğŸ˜Š

06/08/25, 3:34â€¯pm - Vaibhav Pandey: #include <iostream>
#include <cmath>
#include <string>
#include <vector>
using namespace std;

string encryption(string s) {
    // Step 1: Remove spaces
    string clean;
    for (char c : s) {
        if (c != ' ') clean += c;
    }

    int L = clean.size();
    int rows = floor(sqrt(L));
    int cols = ceil(sqrt(L));
    if (rows * cols < L) rows++;

    // Step 2: Fill the grid and build the encrypted message column by column
    string result;
    for (int c = 0; c < cols; ++c) {
        for (int r = 0; r < rows; ++r) {
            int index = r * cols + c;
            if (index < L)
                result += clean[index];
        }
        result += ' ';
    }

    // Remove trailing space
    if (!result.empty() && result.back() == ' ')
        result.pop_back();

    return result;
}

int main() {
    string s;
    getline(cin, s);

    cout << encryption(s) << endl;

    return 0;
}
06/08/25, 3:35â€¯pm - Vaibhav Pandey: #include <iostream>
#include <unordered_map>
#include <string>
#include <algorithm>
using namespace std;

int sherlockAndAnagrams(const string& s) {
    unordered_map<string, int> substrCount;
    int n = s.length();

    // Generate all substrings
    for (int len = 1; len < n; ++len) { // length of substrings
        for (int i = 0; i + len <= n; ++i) {
            string sub = s.substr(i, len);
            sort(sub.begin(), sub.end()); // sorted substrings act as anagram signature
            substrCount[sub]++;
        }
    }

    int result = 0;
    // Count pairs for each group of anagrams
    for (const auto& pair : substrCount) {
        int count = pair.second;
        result += (count * (count - 1)) / 2; // nC2 pairs
    }

    return result;
}

int main() {
    int q;
    cin >> q;
    while (q--) {
        string s;
        cin >> s;
        cout << sherlockAndAnagrams(s) << endl;
    }
    return 0;
}

using namespace std;

string ltrim(const string &);
string rtrim(const string &);
vector<string> split(const string &);

/*
 * Complete the 'largestPermutation' function below.
 *
 * The function is expected to return an INTEGER_ARRAY.
 * The function accepts following parameters:
 *  1. INTEGER k
 *  2. INTEGER_ARRAY arr
 */

vector<int> largestPermutation(int k, vector<int> arr) {

}

int main()
{
    ofstream fout(getenv("OUTPUT_PATH"));

    string first_multiple_input_temp;
    getline(cin, first_multiple_input_temp);

    vector<string> first_multiple_input = split(rtrim(first_multiple_input_temp));

    int n = stoi(first_multiple_input[0]);

    int k = stoi(first_multiple_input[1]);

    string arr_temp_temp;
    getline(cin, arr_temp_temp);

    vector<string> arr_temp = split(rtrim(arr_temp_temp));

    vector<int> arr(n);

    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        int arr_item = stoi(arr_temp[i]);

        arr[i] = arr_item;
    }

    vector<int> result = largestPermutation(k, arr);

    for (size_t i = 0; i < result.size(); i++) {
        fout << result[i];

        if (i != result.size() - 1) {
            fout << " ";
        }
    }

    fout << "\n";

    fout.close();

    return 0;
}

string ltrim(const string &str) {
    string s(str);

    s.erase(
        s.begin(),
        find_if(s.begin(), s.end(), not1(ptr_fun<int, int>(isspace)))
    );

    return s;
}

string rtrim(const string &str) {
    string s(str);

    s.erase(
        find_if(s.rbegin(), s.rend(), not1(ptr_fun<int, int>(isspace))).base(),
        s.end()
    );

    return s;
}

vector<string> split(const string &str) {
    vector<string> tokens;

    string::size_type start = 0;
    string::size_type end = 0;

    while ((end = str.find(" ", start)) != string::npos) {
        tokens.push_back(str.substr(start, end - start));

        start = end + 1;
    }

    tokens.push_back(str.substr(start));

    return tokens;
}
